6.1 ه†’و³،وژ’ه؛ڈ

public class BubbleSort {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {89,75,50,65,40};
        bubbleSort(arr);
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr));
    }

    /**
     * ه†’و³،وژ’ه؛ڈ
     * @param nums ه¾…وژ’ه؛ڈçڑ„و•°ç»„
     */
    public static void bubbleSort(int[] nums){
        int len = nums.length;
        if(nums == null || len<2)
            return;
        for (int i = 0; i < len-1; i++) {
            boolean flag = true;
            for(int j = 0; j < len-i-1; j++){
                if(nums[j] > nums[j+1]){
                    int temp = nums[j];
                    nums[j] = nums[j+1];
                    nums[j+1] = temp;
                    flag = false;
                }
            }
            if(flag){
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

6.2 é€‰و‹©وژ’ه؛ڈ

public class SelectSort {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {89,75,50,65,40};
        selectSort(arr);
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr));
    }
    
    public static void selectSort(int[] arr){
        int len = arr.length;
        if(arr == null || len<2)
            return;
        for(int i=0;i<len;i++){
            int index = i;
            for (int j = i+1; j < len; j++) {
                if(arr[j] < arr[index]){
                    index = j;
                }
            }
            if(index != i)
                swap(arr,i,index);
        }
    }

    public static void swap(int[] arr,int i,int j){
        int temp = arr[i];
        arr[i] = arr[j];
        arr[j] = temp;
    }
}

6.3 وڈ’ه…¥وژ’ه؛ڈ

public class InsertSort {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {2,1,3,4,5};
        insertSort(arr);
        System.out.println(Arrays.toString(arr));
    }

    public static void insertSort(int[] arr){
        int len = arr.length;
        if(arr == null || len<2){
            return;
        }
        for (int i = 1; i < len; i++) {
            int cur = arr[i];
            for (int j = i-1; j >= 0; j--) {
                //è¶…ه‡؛و•°ç»„ه؛•
                if(j==0 && cur<arr[0]){
                    for (int k = i-1; k >= 0; k--) {
                        arr[k+1] = arr[k];
                    }
                    arr[0] = cur;
                }
                if(cur < arr[j] && cur > arr[j-1]){
                    for (int k = i-1; k >= j; k--) {
                        arr[k+1] = arr[k];
                    }
                    arr[j] = cur;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

6.4 وٹکهچٹوں¥و‰¾

public class BinarySearch {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {-45,-35,-20,-10,1,20,23,34,45,50,56};
        int index = search(arr, 34);
        System.out.println(index);
    }

    public static int search(int[] arr,int target){
        int start = 0;
        int end = arr.length-1;
        while (start<=end){
            int mid = (start+end)/2;
            if(target < arr[mid] )
                end = mid-1;
            else if(target > arr[mid]){
                start = mid+1;
            }else{
                return mid;
            }
        }
        return -1;
    }
}

6.5.3 ن»£ç په®‍çژ°و‌¨è¾‰ن¸‰è§’ه½¢ï¼ں

public static void main(String[] args) {
    int len = 7;
    int[][] arr = new int[len][];
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        arr[i] = new int[i+1];
        for(int j=0; j<=i; j++){
            if (j==0 || i==j) {
                arr[i][j] = 1;
            }else{
                arr[i][j] = arr[i-1][j] + arr[i-1][j-1];
            }
        }
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < arr[i].length; j++) {
            System.out.print(arr[i][j]+"\t");
        }
        System.out.println();
    }
}

        //ه±€éƒ¨هڈکé‡ڈ

    public int num=30;
    public int num2=20;

        int num=60;
        System.out.println(num);//ه±€éƒ¨هڈکé‡ڈ  60

    class A{
    double f(double x, double y){
        return x+y;
    }
    
    static int g(int n){
        return n*n;
    }
}

class B extends A{
    double f(double x, double y){
        double m = super.f(x, y);
        return m+x*y;
    }
    static int g(int n){
        int m = A.g(n);
        return m+n;
    }
}

public class E{
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        B b = new B();
        System.out.println(b.f(10.0, 8.0));  //98.0
        System.out.println(b.g(3));  //12
        A a = new B();
        System.out.println(a.f(10.0, 8.0));  //98.0
        System.out.println(a.g(3));  //9
    }
}

11.3 Objectç±»

  • equals()

    • ==

      ه¦‚و‍œ==وک¯هں؛وœ¬و•°وچ®ç±»ه‍‹و¯”è¾ƒçڑ„وک¯ه€¼
ه¦‚و‍œ==وک¯ه¼•ç”¨و•°وچ®ç±»ه‍‹و¯”è¾ƒçڑ„وک¯هœ°ه‌€

    • equals:
      xml é»کè®¤و¯”è¾ƒçڑ„وک¯هœ°ه‌€ وˆ‘ن»¬هڈ¯ن»¥é‡چه†™è®©ه®ƒو¯”è¾ƒوˆگه‘کهڈکé‡ڈçڑ„ه€¼ 

    @Override
public boolean equals(Object obj) {
    if (this == obj)  // هœ°ه‌€ç›¸هگŒï¼ŒوŒ‡هگ‘هگŒن¸€ن¸ھه¯¹è±،
        return true;
    if (obj == null)
        return false;
    if (getClass() != obj.getClass())  //ن¸چه±‍ن؛ژهگŒن¸€ن¸ھç±»çڑ„ه¯¹è±،
        return false;
    Student other = (Student) obj;
    if (age != other.age)
        return false;
    if (name == null) {
        if (other.name != null)
            return false;
    } else if (!name.equals(other.name))
        return false;
    return true;
}

    public class DiGuiDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // هˆ›ه»؛Fileه¯¹è±،
        File dir  = new File("D:\\aaa");
          // è°ƒç”¨و‰“هچ°ç›®ه½•و–¹و³•

    }

    public static void printDir(File dir) {
          // èژ·هڈ–ه­گو–‡ن»¶ه’Œç›®ه½•
        File[] files = dir.listFiles();
          // ه¾ھçژ¯و‰“هچ°
        for (File file : files) {
            if (file.isFile()) {
                  // وک¯و–‡ن»¶ï¼Œهˆ¤و–­و–‡ن»¶هگچه¹¶è¾“ه‡؛و–‡ن»¶ç»‌ه¯¹è·¯ه¾„
                if (file.getName().endsWith(".java")) {
                    System.out.println("و–‡ن»¶هگچ:" + file.getAbsolutePath());
                }
            } else {
                // وک¯ç›®ه½•ï¼Œç»§ç»­éپچهژ†,ه½¢وˆگé€’ه½’
                printDir(file);
            }
        }
    }
}

public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        File file = new File("D:\\Java\\jdk1.8.0_121");
        getFile(file);
    }

    /**
     * @param file è¦پéپچهژ†çڑ„و–‡ن»¶ه¤¹
     */
    public static void getFile(File file){
        //èژ·هڈ–ه½“ه‰چو–‡ن»¶ه¤¹ن¸‹و‰€وœ‰çڑ„و–‡ن»¶هڈٹه­گو–‡ن»¶
        File[] listFiles = file.listFiles(new FileFilter() {
            @Override
            public boolean accept(File pathname) {
                if(pathname.getName().endsWith(".java"))
                    return true;
                //و–‡ن»¶ه¤¹è¦پéپچهژ†ه‡؛و‌¥
                if(pathname.isDirectory())
                    return true;
                return false;
            }
        });
        for(File f : listFiles){
            //ه¦‚و‍œوک¯و–‡ن»¶ه¤¹هˆ™é€’ه½’éپچهژ†
            if(f.isDirectory()){
                getFile(f);
            }else{
                System.out.println(f.getName());
            }
        }
    }
}

public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        File file = new File("D:\\Java\\jdk1.8.0_121");
        getFile(file);
    }

    /**
     * @param file è¦پéپچهژ†çڑ„و–‡ن»¶ه¤¹
     */

        //èژ·هڈ–ه½“ه‰چو–‡ن»¶ه¤¹ن¸‹و‰€وœ‰çڑ„و–‡ن»¶هڈٹه­گو–‡ن»¶
        File[] listFiles = file.listFiles(pathname -> {
            if(pathname.getName().endsWith(".java"))
                return true;
            if(pathname.isDirectory())
                return true;
            return false;
        });
        for(File f : listFiles){
            //ه¦‚و‍œوک¯و–‡ن»¶ه¤¹هˆ™é€’ه½’éپچهژ†
            if(f.isDirectory()){
                getFile(f);
            }else{
                //if(f.getName().endsWith(".java"))
                System.out.println(f.getName());
            }
        }
    }
}

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sum(1,2));
        System.out.println(sum(1,2,3));
        System.out.println(sum(new int[]{1,2,3,4}));
    }

    public static int sum(int ...num){
        int sum = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < num.length; i++) {
            sum += num[i];
        }
        return sum;
    }
}

ArrayList(int initialCapacity) 
          و‍„é€ ن¸€ن¸ھه…·وœ‰وŒ‡ه®ڑهˆ‌ه§‹ه®¹é‡ڈçڑ„ç©؛هˆ—è،¨م€‚

//è‡ھهٹ¨و‰©ه®¹çڑ„ن»£ç پ
private Object[] grow(int minCapacity) {
    //è€پو•°ç»„çڑ„é•؟ه؛¦
    int oldCapacity = elementData.length;

    //ن½ ن¸چوک¯ç©؛çڑ„و•°ç»„ه°±و‰§è،Œifن¸­çڑ„ن»£ç پ
    if (oldCapacity > 0 || elementData != DEFAULTCAPACITY_EMPTY_ELEMENTDATA) {

        //newCapacityو–°çڑ„ه®¹é‡ڈ 
        int newCapacity = ArraysSupport.newLength(oldCapacity,
                                                  minCapacity - oldCapacity, /* minimum growth */
                                                  oldCapacity >> 1           /* preferred growth */);

        // >> ن½چè؟گç®—  هڈ³ç§»ن¸€ن½چ هڈ³ç§»ن¸€ن½چç›¸ه½“ن؛ژé™¤2
        //و‰©ه®¹1.5ه€چ
        oldCapacity+oldCapacity >> 1 

            //و–°çڑ„و•°ç»„é•؟ه؛¦وک¯15  è€پçڑ„و•°ç»„é•؟ه؛¦وک¯10  éœ€è¦پوٹٹè€پçڑ„و•°ç»„çڑ„و•°وچ®ه¤چهˆ¶هˆ°و–°çڑ„و•°ç»„
            return elementData = Arrays.copyOf(elementData, newCapacity);

    } else {
        return elementData = new Object[Math.max(DEFAULT_CAPACITY, minCapacity)];
    }
}

15.2 Set

java.util.HashSetوک¯Setوژ¥هڈ£çڑ„ن¸€ن¸ھه®‍çژ°ç±»ï¼Œه®ƒو‰€ه­که‚¨çڑ„ه…ƒç´ وک¯ن¸چهڈ¯é‡چه¤چçڑ„ï¼Œه¹¶ن¸”ه…ƒç´ éƒ½وک¯و— ه؛ڈçڑ„(هچ³ه­کهڈ–é،؛ه؛ڈن¸چن¸€è‡´)م€‚java.util.HashSetه؛•ه±‚çڑ„ه®‍çژ°ه…¶ه®‍وک¯ن¸€ن¸ھjava.util.HashMapو”¯وŒپم€‚

HashSetوک¯و ¹وچ®ه¯¹è±،çڑ„ه“ˆه¸Œه€¼و‌¥ç،®ه®ڑه…ƒç´ هœ¨é›†هگˆن¸­çڑ„ه­که‚¨ن½چç½®ï¼Œه› و­¤ه…·وœ‰è‰¯ه¥½çڑ„ه­کهڈ–ه’Œوں¥و‰¾و€§èƒ½م€‚ن؟‌è¯په…ƒç´ ه”¯ن¸€و€§çڑ„و–¹ه¼ڈن¾‌èµ–ن؛ژï¼ڑhashCodeن¸ژequalsو–¹و³•م€‚

15.2.1 ه­که‚¨è‡ھه®ڑن¹‰ه¯¹è±،é—®é¢ک

  • é»کè®¤çڑ„hashCodeه°±وک¯ه†…ه­کهœ°ه‌€ï¼Œوˆگه‘کهڈکé‡ڈه€¼ç›¸هگŒçڑ„ه¯¹è±،ن¹ںن¼ڑه¯¼è‡´ه…¶hashcodeن¸چن¸€و ·

  • ه¦‚و‍œن¸¤ن¸ھه¯¹è±،çڑ„و‰€وœ‰çڑ„وˆگه‘کهڈکé‡ڈن¸€è‡´ï¼Œوˆ‘ن»¬ه؛”è¯¥è®©hashCodeن¸€è‡´

  • ن¸؛ن؛†ن؟‌è¯پSeté›†هگˆه…ƒç´ ن¸چé‡چه¤چçڑ„ç‰¹و€§ï¼Œè¦پé‡چه†™è‡ھه®ڑن¹‰ç±»çڑ„hashcode()ه’Œequals()و–¹و³•

public class Student {
    private String name;
    
    private Integer age;
    
    public Student() {
        
    }
    
    public Student(String name, Integer age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    
    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }
    
    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }
    
    public Integer getAge() {
        return age;
    }
    
    public void setAge(Integer age) {
        this.age = age;
    }
    
    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student [name=" + name + ", age=" + age + "]";
    }
    
    //ه¦‚و‍œè¦پç”¨seté›†هگˆè؟›è،Œه­که‚¨ï¼Œé‡چه†™çڑ„hashCodeو–¹و³•
    //هڈھè¦پوˆگه‘کهڈکé‡ڈçڑ„ه€¼وک¯ç›¸هگŒçڑ„ï¼Œè®،ç®—çڑ„hashCodeçڑ„ه€¼ه°±وک¯ç›¸هگŒçڑ„
    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        final int prime = 31;
        int result = 1;
        result = prime * result + ((age == null) ? 0 : age.hashCode());
        result = prime * result + ((name == null) ? 0 : name.hashCode());
        return result;
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object obj) {
        if (this == obj)
            return true;
        if (obj == null)
            return false;
        if (getClass() != obj.getClass())
            return false;
        Student other = (Student) obj;
        if (age == null) {
            if (other.age != null)
                return false;
        } else if (!age.equals(other.age))
            return false;
        if (name == null) {
            if (other.name != null)
                return false;
        } else if (!name.equals(other.name))
            return false;
        return true;
    }
}

16.1.3 Keyن¸؛è‡ھه®ڑن¹‰ه¯¹è±،

public class Student {
    private String name;

    private int age;

    public Student() {
    }

    public Student(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) {
            return true;
        }
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) {
            return false;
        }
        Student student = (Student) o;
        return age == student.age &&
                Objects.equals(name, student.name);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}

public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Map<Student,Integer> map = new HashMap<>();
        map.put(new Student("aaa",22),1);
        map.put(new Student("bbb",24),2);
        map.put(new Student("aaa",22),3);
        map.put(new Student("ddd",26),4);

        System.out.println(map);
    }
}
  • Mapçڑ„keyوک¯ه”¯ن¸€çڑ„ï¼Œن¸؛ن؛†ن؟‌è¯پkeyçڑ„ه”¯ن¸€و€§ï¼Œè¦پé‡چه†™è‡ھه®ڑن¹‰ç±»çڑ„hashCode()ه’Œequalsو–¹و³•

  • HashMapçڑ„ه­گç±»

  • ه¹¶è،Œï¼ڑوŒ‡ن¸¤ن¸ھوˆ–ه¤ڑن¸ھن؛‹ن»¶هœ¨هگŒن¸€و—¶هˆ»هڈ‘ç”ںï¼ˆهگŒو—¶هڈ‘ç”ںï¼‰

16.2.2 è؟›ç¨‹ن¸ژç؛؟ç¨‹(é‌¢è¯•é¢ک)

public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //هˆ›ه»؛ç؛؟ç¨‹
        Thread thread = new Thread(new Runnable() {
            @Override
            public void run() {
                for (int i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
                    System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"_"+i);
                }
            }
        });

        thread.start();

        for (int i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
            System.out.println("Main_"+i);
        }
    }
}

public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //هˆ›ه»؛ç؛؟ç¨‹
        Thread thread = new Thread(() -> {
            for (int i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
                System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"_"+i);
            }
        });

        thread.start();

        for (int i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
            System.out.println("Main_"+i);
        }
    }
}

            System.out.println("Main_"+i);
        }
    }
}

        Thread t = new Thread(mt);

class MyThread implements Runnable{
    //ه†™ه¸ƒه°”و ‡è®°
    boolean run = true;
    
    @Override
    public void run() {
        for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
            if(run){//true و‰§è،Œç؛؟ç¨‹ن»»هٹ،
                System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"---"+i);
                try {
                    Thread.sleep(1000);
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
            }else{
                //false ç»ˆو­¢ه½“ه‰چç؛؟ç¨‹=ç»ˆو­¢run()و–¹و³•
                return;
            }
        }
    }
}

17.1.6ç؛؟ç¨‹و‰§è،Œوœ‰é،؛ه؛ڈ

  • public final void join() throws InterruptedException

    • è¯¥و–¹و³•هڈ¯ن»¥هچڈè°ƒç؛؟ç¨‹ن¹‹é—´çڑ„هگŒو­¥è؟گè،Œ
    public class ThreadDemo06 {
    private static boolean isFinish = false;
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //1.ن¸‹è½½ç؛؟ç¨‹
        Thread download = new Thread(new Runnable() {
        
            @Override
            public void run() {
                System.out.println("download:ه¼€ه§‹ن¸‹è½½ه›¾ç‰‡....");
                for (int i = 1; i <=100; i++) {
                    System.out.println("download:"+i+"%");
                    try {
                        Thread.sleep(40);
                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                        e.printStackTrace();
                    }
                }
                isFinish = true;
            }
        });
        
        //2.وک¾ç¤؛ç؛؟ç¨‹
        Thread show = new Thread(new Runnable() {
            
            @Override
            public void run() {
                try {
                    /*
                     * showç؛؟ç¨‹هٹ هˆ°downloadç؛؟ç¨‹هگژé‌¢ï¼ڑ
                     * هœ¨showç؛؟ç¨‹ن¸­è°ƒç”¨download.join();ï¼Œو­¤و—¶showç؛؟ç¨‹
                     * ه¤„ن؛ژéک»ه،‍çٹ¶و€پï¼Œç›´هˆ°downloadو‰§è،Œه®Œو¯•showç؛؟ç¨‹è§£é™¤éک»ه،‍
                     * ه¼€ه§‹و‰§è،Œï¼پï¼پï¼پ
                     */
                    download.join();
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
                System.out.println("show:وک¾ç¤؛ه›¾ç‰‡");
                if(!isFinish){
                    throw new RuntimeException("هٹ è½½ه›¾ç‰‡ه¤±è´¥");
                }
            }
        });
        
        //3.è؟گè،Œ
        download.start();
        show.start();
    }
}

17.4.3 Locké”پ

  • java.util.concurrent.locks.Lock وœ؛هˆ¶وڈگن¾›ن؛†و¯”synchronizedن»£ç په‌—ه’Œsynchronizedو–¹و³•و›´ه¹؟و³›çڑ„é”په®ڑو“چن½œ,هگŒو­¥ن»£ç په‌—/هگŒو­¥و–¹و³•ه…·وœ‰çڑ„هٹںèƒ½Lockéƒ½وœ‰,é™¤و­¤ن¹‹ه¤–و›´ه¼؛ه¤§,و›´ن½“çژ°é‌¢هگ‘ه¯¹è±،م€‚
  • Locké”پن¹ںç§°هگŒو­¥é”پï¼Œهٹ é”پن¸ژé‡ٹو”¾é”پو–¹و³•هŒ–ن؛†ï¼Œه¦‚ن¸‹ï¼ڑ
    • public void lock() :هٹ هگŒو­¥é”پم€‚
    • public void unlock() :é‡ٹو”¾هگŒو­¥é”پم€‚
public class Ticket extends Thread{
    private int ticket = 100;
    
    private Lock lock = new ReentrantLock();
    
    @Override
    public void run() {
        while(ticket>0){
            //1.èژ·ه¾—é”پ
            lock.lock();
            System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"و­£هœ¨ه”®ç¥¨:"+ticket--);
            try {
                Thread.sleep(200);
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
            //2.é‡ٹو”¾é”پ
            lock.unlock();
        }
    }
}

class MyThread1 extends Thread{
    Object o1;//هگŒو­¥é”پ1
    Object o2;//هگŒو­¥é”پ2

        this.o1 = o1;
        this.o2 = o2;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void run() {
        synchronized (o1) {

                Thread.sleep(1000);
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
            synchronized (o2) {
                
            }
        }
    }
}

18.3 ç”ںن؛§è€…ن¸ژو¶ˆè´¹è€…

  • wait()ه’Œnotify()و–¹و³•çڑ„ن½؟ç”¨و‌،ن»¶
    • Objectن¸­çڑ„و–¹و³•
    • wait()ه’Œnotify()و–¹و³•ه؟…é،»ç”±هگŒن¸€ن¸ھé”په¯¹è±،è°ƒç”¨
    • wait()ه’Œnotify()و–¹و³•ه؟…é،»ن½؟ç”¨هœ¨هگŒو­¥و–¹و³•/هگŒو­¥ن»£ç په‌—ن¸­
public class ProCon {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        List<Object> list = new ArrayList<Object>();
        Producer producer = new Producer(list);
        Consumer consumer = new Consumer(list);
        
        Thread t1 = new Thread(producer,"ç”ںن؛§ç؛؟ç¨‹");
        Thread t2 = new Thread(consumer,"و¶ˆè´¹ç؛؟ç¨‹");
        
        t1.start();
        t2.start();
    }

}

class Producer implements Runnable{
    private List<Object> list;
    
    public Producer(List<Object> list) {
        this.list = list;
    }

    @Override
    public void run() {
        while(true){
            synchronized (list) {
                //وœ‰و•°وچ®
                if(list.size()>0){
                    try {
                        list.wait();
                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                        e.printStackTrace();
                    }
                }
                //و²،وœ‰و•°وچ®
                Object object = new Object();
                try {
                    Thread.sleep(1000);
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
                list.add(object);
                System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"ç”ںن؛§ن¸€ن¸ھو•°وچ®"+object);
                list.notify();
            }
        }
    }
}

class Consumer implements Runnable{
    private List<Object> list;
    
    public Consumer(List<Object> list) {
        this.list = list;
    }

    @Override
    public void run() {
        while(true){
            synchronized (list) {
                if(list.size()==0){
                    try {
                        list.wait();
                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                        e.printStackTrace();
                    }
                }
                Object object = list.remove(0);
                try {
                    Thread.sleep(1000);
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
                System.out.println(Thread.currentThread().getName()+"و¶ˆè´¹ن¸€ن¸ھو•°وچ®"+object);
                list.notify();
            }
        }
    }
}

18.4 ç­‰ه¾…ه”¤é†’وœ؛هˆ¶

19.2.1 Supplier

ç”ںن؛§وژ¥هڈ£هŒ…هگ«ن¸€ن¸ھو— هڈ‚وœ‰è؟”ه›‍ه€¼çڑ„و–¹و³•ï¼ڑT get(); èژ·هڈ–وŒ‡ه®ڑو³›ه‍‹ç±»ه‍‹çڑ„و•°وچ®

public class SupplierDemo {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        getString(() -> "JAVA");
    }
    

    public static void getString(Supplier<String> s){
        String string = s.get();
        System.out.println(string);
    }

}

19.2.2 Consumer

و¶ˆè´¹وژ¥هڈ£ï¼ŒهŒ…هگ«ن¸€ن¸ھوœ‰هڈ‚و²،وœ‰è؟”ه›‍ه€¼çڑ„و–¹و³•ï¼ڑvoid accept(T t);

public class ConsumerDemo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        setString("JAVA", (str) -> {
            String s = "HELLO,"+str;
            System.out.println(s);
            });
    }
    
    public static void setString(String str, Consumer<String> c){
        c.accept(str);
    }
}

19.2.3 Predicate

هˆ¤و–­/وµ‹è¯•وژ¥هڈ£ï¼ŒهŒ…هگ«ن¸€ن¸ھوœ‰هڈ‚وœ‰è؟”ه›‍ه€¼çڑ„و–¹و³•ï¼ڑboolean test(T t)

public static void main(String[] args) {
    boolean flag = testStr("HELLO,JAVA", str -> {
        return str.contains("JVA");
    });
    System.out.println(flag);
}

public static boolean testStr(String str,Predicate<String> p){
    boolean flag = p.test(str);
    return flag;
}

19.2.4 Function

è½¬وچ¢هٹںèƒ½وژ¥هڈ£ï¼ŒهŒ…هگ«ن¸€ن¸ھوœ‰هڈ‚وœ‰è؟”ه›‍ه€¼çڑ„و–¹و³•ï¼ڑR apply(T t)

public static void main(String[] args) {
    converse("1234", (str) -> Integer.parseInt(str));
}

public static void converse(String str,Function<String, Integer> f){
    Integer num = f.apply(str);
    System.out.println(num);
}

public static void main(String[] args) {
    List<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
    Collections.addAll(list,1,5,4,3,6,8,2,7);
    Stream<Integer> stream = list.stream();

    stream.sorted().forEach(num -> System.out.println(num));
    stream.sorted((a,b) -> b-a).forEach(num -> System.out.print(num));
}

20.5.2 Propertiesç±»

  • و‍„é€ و–¹و³•ï¼ڑ

      public static void main(String[] args) throws FileNotFoundException {
    // هˆ›ه»؛ه±‍و€§é›†ه¯¹è±،
    Properties properties = new Properties();
    // و·»هٹ é”®ه€¼ه¯¹ه…ƒç´ 
    properties.setProperty("filename", "a.txt");
    properties.setProperty("length", "209385038");
    properties.setProperty("location", "D:\\a.txt");
    // و‰“هچ°ه±‍و€§é›†ه¯¹è±،
    System.out.println(properties);
    // é€ڑè؟‡é”®,èژ·هڈ–ه±‍و€§ه€¼
    System.out.println(properties.getProperty("filename"));
    System.out.println(properties.getProperty("length"));
    System.out.println(properties.getProperty("location"));
    // éپچهژ†ه±‍و€§é›†,èژ·هڈ–و‰€وœ‰é”®çڑ„é›†هگˆ
    Set<String> strings = properties.stringPropertyNames();
    // و‰“هچ°é”®ه€¼ه¯¹
    for (String key : strings ) {
        System.out.println(key+" -- "+properties.getProperty(key));
    }
}

      public class DeserializeDemo {
   public static void main(String [] args)   {
        Employee e = null;
        try {		
             // هˆ›ه»؛هڈچه؛ڈهˆ—هŒ–وµپ
             FileInputStream fileIn = new FileInputStream("employee.txt");

        System.out.println("Address: " + e.address); // beiqinglu
        System.out.println("age: " + e.age); // 0
    }
}

public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException, ClassNotFoundException {
    //ه†™
    ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
    BufferedOutputStream bos = new BufferedOutputStream(baos);
    ObjectOutputStream oos = new ObjectOutputStream(bos);
    oos.writeInt(123);
    oos.writeDouble(3.14);
    oos.writeChar('A');
    oos.writeObject(new Date());
    //هˆ·و–°وµپï¼ڑه†™ه…¥و•°وچ®هگژè®°ه¾—هˆ·و–°ï¼پï¼پï¼پ
    oos.flush();

    //èژ·هڈ–و•°وچ®
    byte[] bs = baos.toByteArray();

    //è¯»
    ByteArrayInputStream bais = new ByteArrayInputStream(bs);
    BufferedInputStream bis = new BufferedInputStream(bais);
    ObjectInputStream ois = new ObjectInputStream(bis);

    //è¯»هڈ–و•°وچ®
    int i = ois.readInt();
    double d = ois.readDouble();
    char ch = ois.readChar();
    Object obj = ois.readObject();

    System.out.println(i+"-"+d+"-"+obj+"-"+ch);

    //é‡ٹو”¾وµپ
}

public class Test {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //هˆ¤و–­وک¯هگ¦ه؛”ç”¨ن؛†è¯¥و³¨è§£
